<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fralētaną</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>laten</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlegen.html>verlegen</a> (2816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlegen.html>verlegen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlegen.html>verlegen</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verlegen.html>verlegener</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">verlegenst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:shy.html>shy</a>, bashful, <a href = vnd.unilang:timid.html>timid</a></li>
<li>embarrassed</li>
<li>lacking, having <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shortage.html>shortage</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:spoiled.html>spoiled</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rotten.html>rotten</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verlegen.html>verlegen</a></b>
